Free Talk

A Laughing Matter · Hai · Ke 167

A｜Why does your face look so terrible these past few days? Are you not feeling well?

B｜It's not that, it's because my stepmother is not feeling well.

A｜Is that so? Is it because you are too worried?

B｜It's not that either, it's just because my stepmother has not been feeling well lately and hired a doctor to treat her. According to the doctor, she needs to exercise more every day, so she beats me every day as part of her daily exercise.

A｜Lao Bing has safely arrived in Japan and sent me a telegram yesterday.

B｜Did he suffer on the way?

A｜He didn't suffer because his wife didn't go with him.

Pastor｜Friends, when living in this world, you should always think about the word "live." Give people a way out of the road to death. Living people are the way to live.

Executioner｜Pastor, I'm sorry I can't do this because I am an executioner in the yamen. I often find a way to death for people in the road to life. Killing people can make me live.

Li Liejun and Chen Sanli Compose Poems in Lushan 168

Dou Jun, Mr. Li Xiehe (Liejun) of Jiangxi is a founding hero of the party-state. Since leaving Beijing in the 17th year of the Republic of China and returning to Jiangxi, he has been living in seclusion in his hometown of Wuning, devoting himself to the forests and springs and forgetting about fame and wealth. If asked about party-state affairs, he would smile and talk about other things. Since the summer heat has gradually intensified, Mr. Li went to Lushan to escape the heat a month ago. Lushan is a famous mountain since ancient times. Mr. Li sojourns there, composing poems from time to time. Mr. Chen Sanli, the elder San Yuan of Yining, also came to the mountain to escape the heat. Mr. Li regarded the elder as the greatest poet of the time, treating him with the utmost hospitality and showing him the old poems he had written on a boat in the river. The elder followed the rhyme to reciprocate, and his poem is as follows: (At first, I suspected that I had arrived in Shizhou, and the shade of the pines was deep and the bamboos were tall. I tried my best to collect the soaring energy of Qianmo and connected it to the wandering of Lu Ao. Looking back at my hometown, it has become a den of thieves, so I peacefully live in the springs and rocks. The setting sun is in the clouds on the path, appearing and disappearing like an unmoored boat.) It is indeed a great event that the founding hero of the party-state and the poet of the time composed poems in a famous mountain. Mr. Li's poems have been published in various newspapers, so they are not recorded here. It is also heard that the mountain monk Master Dazhi, who is noble in virtue and proficient in Sanskrit, is also revered by the two gentlemen.

Record of a New Robbery Case in Hangzhou, Zhu Jun 169

Robbery cases have been frequently heard in Hangzhou this month. First, a nunnery outside Wulin Gate was robbed of money by drugging. Then, the Hengda Tobacco Shop was robbed of money and people were killed. Fortunately, the authorities made every effort to investigate and cracked the case soon. Unexpectedly, a similar drugging robbery case occurred at Anji Temple on Jianqiao Bridge a few days ago. It is not unique but exactly the the same. It is really noteworthy that two people were victimized, one died and one fell ill. The details are recorded as follows: The Location and Current Situation of the Temple Jianqiao Street is the center of the city. There is a constant flow of traffic. Shops are adjacent to the road from the city station to the new market. The temple is located in Zhangjiaqiao on the street, and a monk and a Taoist priest live there to preside over the temple. There are two temple keepers, one named Jiang Jucai and the other named Ma Fulin, who are both law-abiding. Recently, a man from Xiaoshan named A Fu, who is 80 years old, came to the temple to stay temporarily. He is well known by the monk. The monk and the temple keepers have some savings from chanting scriptures, which has aroused the covetousness of bandits. The Circumstances of the Robbery On the evening of the 4th, the presiding monk and the temple keeper Ma went out to chant scriptures and only left the temple keeper Jiang and the old man. At about 8:00 PM, there was a loud knock on the door, claiming to be someone who had come to order scriptures. When the door was opened, four men in short clothes rushed in. They asked for two teacups and took out something similar to shortbread from their chests. They mixed it with boiling water and forced the two men to drink it. The people who came also held rosary beads and claimed that this was vegetarian food and told them to drink it with peace of mind. Leftover Poems of Noble Women

New Thoughts on Seedling Pulling, Autumn Water 171

As the weather has been getting hotter recently, when we are in the office every day, we often take off our coats and hang them on the hooks on the wall or place them randomly on the corners of chairs and tables. It can also be said that valuable items are often placed in the pockets of our coats. We sit in the office and never worry about theft within sight. The weather is getting hotter and more people are going to the office without their coats. I don’t know that a group of poor and idle people have actually seen through our habits and implemented their novel seedling pulling techniques. I quickly recorded it to punish the traitors. It is said that this kind of seedling pulling was invented by two White Russians. There have been two incidents to date to prove it. One of them was in a certain foreign firm at No. 21 Yuanmingyuan Road. At around 9:00 AM or 10:00 AM on May 30th, two Westerners, neatly dressed and with generous manners, strolled into the office of the foreign firm. One of them took off his hat and saluted the office staff (note that there was only one person working in the office at this time). The clerk saw that they were noble gentlemen and sincerely entertained them, asking what they wanted. One of the people who came asked for the address of a certain foreign firm. The clerk took out a directory of companies to search for it. I don’t know that while the clerk was concentrating on answering and flipping through the directory, the other person who came was using his quick hands. The clerk’s coat happened to be hanging on the hook behind him. The clerk was sitting in the chair facing the person who asked the question and did not pay attention. In a blink of an eye, the banknotes, numbers of coins and diary were already in the bag of the visitor, and the clerk did not know it. The person asking the question saw that it was done and then said goodbye and left together. The clerk did not know that this uninvited guest was a thief until after get off work. The other was at No. 17 Bowuyuan Road, also a Western foreign firm. The incident was very similar and was probably done by the same gang. Only after entering the room, the conversation was slightly different. It can be seen from the above two incidents that these thieves must be neatly dressed so that people will not be suspicious. The place where they operate must be a place where foreign firms and companies gather, hoping that what they get will be plentiful. The office they visit must be a place where there are very few clerks and where there are clothes hanging on the corners of the wall so that their purpose can be easily achieved without wasting their time. I hope that the readers of the newspaper will pay attention to it.

Special Ways of Eating Chicken, Di Weng 172

Chicken is a delicacy among foods. Unfortunately, ordinary cooking often results in half of the flavor being lost in the soup, and the chicken meat cannot have a particularly good taste. Since last winter, I have been invited to dine by friends and have eaten special foods twice, both of which were chicken. Now I will explain in detail the method of preparing these foods. Although they are not mountain and sea delicacies, they are different from ordinary foods. Air-Dried Chicken with Feathers Kill a young hen weighing two or three pounds, remove its stomach and fill it with salt. Do not remove the feathers and do not put it in water. Use salt on the outside and rub it against the direction of the feathers. After rubbing the salt, hang it in a ventilated place for a month before it can be eaten. When eating, first remove the feathers and then boil water to the boiling point. Then put the chicken in the boiling water and cover the pot. Do not add more fire. After half an hour, take the chicken out and boil the water again until it boils as before. Put the chicken back into the pot and take it out again after half an hour to eat it. The chicken is tender and delicious, and the taste is very different from ordinary chicken. However, this method is suitable for winter. In spring, when the weather is warm, it is easy to spoil. Mud Chicken Also use a young hen weighing two or three pounds. Kill it, remove its stomach, and also do not remove the feathers. Pour salt, wine, soy sauce, and other seasonings into the chicken belly and sew the mouth with thread. Cover it completely with muddy mud, then wrap it with wet grass paper and pile it up with rice husks and burn it with a slow fire for about four hours. When the mud is dry, the chicken is cooked. Throw the chicken away and the feathers will fall off with the mud. The taste is very usable. Wrapping it with wet grass paper can remove the smoky smell. Both methods preserve the true flavor. The latter method is dry-smoked, and although the former method puts it into boiling water, it does not continue to boil, so the true flavor does not escape. It can be used to accompany wine to remove special delicacies.

Warmth in the Heart (221), Bao Tianxiao 173

Chapter Twelve: Farewell Banquet and Leaving Feast, Picking Flowers to Keep Beautiful Shadows, Famous Garden Party, Tasting Tea to See Beautiful Faces. It is said that Ruiyun's wedding date is approaching. Her stepmother, the eldest aunt, has been coaxing her these days like coaxing a child. She is simply saying how good the Zhang family is, how all these things are your good fortune, no one can take it away from you. Now, which of the sisters doesn't envy you? She also said that when you go out, I will also make you some beautiful clothes. I have already made you a pink embroidered padded jacket and a pink embroidered skirt. You have never worn a skirt in your life. This is also the first time. It is also your good fortune to wear a red skirt for the first time. You must know that in the large mansion, you are not allowed to wear a red skirt as a concubine. You can only wear colored skirts unless you have a son. Only when the young master is getting married can his biological mother come out to pay her respects before she can wear a red skirt, and she must also get the consent of the wife and the permission of the master. Now I tell Young Master Zhang that he says whatever you want, anyway, I don't have a wife. If the old lady knows about it, she won't agree. It's good to keep it from her. Do you think how generous and lucky he is? Although the pink skirt is a little worse than wearing a bright red skirt, what about the new-style free marriage nowadays? You have also seen people formally getting married in civilized dramas, and the bride is also wearing that set of clothes. I made this set of brightly colored clothes for you, which also cost dozens of yuan. In fact, she was reluctant to pay for it herself. She received all 5,000 yuan and was unwilling to lose any money to make clothes for her. She cleverly requested Zhang's family to pay another sum of money. She said that now that the person is your person, even making clothes is what your people wear and is what you should do. It is also your face to wear some beautiful clothes when you go to your mansion. Since Young Master Zhang likes Ruiyun, how can he refuse? The Zhang family was originally a large family in Wujun and treated people kindly, which is not like some official families who have certain rules for taking concubines. It is said that at that time, there was a master who was also a very high official, but he had a lot of internal pets and more than a dozen concubines. Although he had so many concubines, he still wanted to prostitute. Fortunately, there are prostitutes everywhere in China. In Beijing and Tianjin, they call it "going to the kiln," and in Shanghai and Suzhou, they call it "going to the brothel." This master is very happy and doesn't put on airs when he goes to the brothel. He has the best temper and is the first to be confused. The girls in the brothel want him to stand, so he stands, and if they want him to kneel, he kneels. If he wants to please you, he can agree to any conditions you propose. They were originally a family of scholars, and the girls thought that marrying this master must be satisfactory.

Grain and Rice Market Quiet but Firm 183

Zhabei: The source market sales vary. Beigeng has large-scale exits and entries. The retail sales in the four townships are lively. The supply of high-quality Zhongguan goods is tight. However, recently, foreign rice has become popular. Common people in Dabu are shifting their attention to foreign rice because the price of geng is too high. Therefore, the sales of geng declined and prices frequently decreased last week. In reality, it is difficult to return to small quantities during this transition period. Yesterday afternoon, the market was extremely firm and slightly increased due to people's sentiments. Thin and stable sales, stable prices, and slight changes. The continued sales of Huhang white geng from Subutong were firm. Businessmen were thin, and early gains were not good. All are set on Yangxian Duzixian. Sales in the market are mainly Xigong minor. Yuan Yin Hua is still mediocre.

Flour Market Rebounds After Covering Short Positions 184

Yesterday, the flour market saw rising prices in both the upper and lower markets after opening. The opening price in the front market was very soft. However, manufacturers secretly stopped selling to cover short positions, and new bulls became active again, causing prices to rise sequentially. The current month rose to 2 taels 5 qian 7 fen and a half, and November rose to 2 taels 5 qian 4 fen 25. The closing market rebounded slightly by 25. Compared to the previous day's closing market, the 680th month was up 1.7 fen, the 7th month was up half a fen, the 9th month was up 7 li 5, and the 11th month was up 2 fen. The market situation is still showing a rebound.

Wheat Prices: Old Wheat Rises, New Wheat Flat 185

Standard Returns Small: Yesterday, the wheat futures market showed a flat and weak trend for all months. This was because the new wheat arrived in abundance, and everyone unanimously returned to small quantities. After this, if the arrival volume increases again, the market may temporarily stabilize. The closing prices were: June, down 2 fen; July, down 1.89 fen; September, down 3 fen; October, down 2 fen; November, down 1 fen. New wheat arrival volume was very high. The volume of old wheat was also high. However, the factory demand for high-quality old wheat was very strong. 7,000 bags of Qingjiangpu Shenwan wheat were opened at a price of 5 taels 3 qian, an increase of 5 fen. 18,000 to 9,000 bags of new wheat arrived, and 10,000 bags were sold. The market was flat. The opening prices were: Lai Kunshan wheat, 4 taels 9 qian 4 fen; Baoshan wheat, 4 taels 8 qian 7 fen; Pudong wheat, 4 taels 7 qian; Puzhen wheat, 4 taels 9 qian; Nanjing wheat, 4 taels 8 qian 2 fen.

Foreign Rice: Sharp Rises and Falls 186

Up and Down by One Jiao: Yesterday, the sales of foreign rice were more active. The total market opened with 17,000 to 8,000 bags. The market had a strong appetite, and high-quality goods were particularly sought after. Therefore, high-quality goods immediately rose by one jiao. However, the number of medium and lower-quality goods arriving was too high in recent days. Therefore, lower-quality goods decreased by one jiao. The goods sold in the general market were all purchased by the local market, with only a small number purchased by foreign markets.

Silk and Tea: Overseas New Silk Telegram Prices Remain Small 187

Yesterday, the silk market in this port seemed to be starting. New factories in New York have wired that the Shanghai Qianli Sanjing and other companies have invited Chinese silk merchants to negotiate. The increase in silk prices is very small. The factory is still short of silk, so it is difficult to reach an agreement. Transactions are waiting for new ones to come. Companies such as Dachang have negotiated, but the selling price is not high, and the owners do not announce it.

New York has a Total of 58,000 Bales of Raw Silk 188

Since the summer, the sales of silk fabrics in the New York market have been sluggish. The factory sales of raw silk materials have decreased sharply, mostly being replaced by rayon. Imports of raw silk from various countries have decreased sharply, but the inventory is still high. According to a telegram from the New York Silk Association, New York warehouses have a total of 58,000 bales of raw silk from China, Japan, China, and France, which is sufficient for several months of demand.

Russian Firm's Tea Purchasing Policy 189

Since Russian tea master Wu Ji Luofu arrived in Shanghai, the Chinese tea market has been in a slump. Chinese tea merchants attach great importance to the merchant's attitude. According to Russian sources, since the suspension last year, Russia does not have much tea in stock. The market is reorganizing, but the price of Qimen black tea is too expensive and does not meet sales needs. Zhuangzhen eyebrow Gongxi has considerable needs. The process will be reorganized and opened. However, the firm adheres to the principle of only buying if the price is cheap, and Gongxi with tea seeds are also rejected.

Dried Goods: Xingzheng Er Guifei is Out of Stock 190

Yesterday, each line of hand goods were sold out. The price is up 56 Liang from before. It is still far from the release of new goods. The late market is preventing more tension. Lu Shangdang Yuan is now slightly looser due to the time limit, with a few cents to one or two fluctuations from the previous day.

Friday (3rd) Huge Losses in the Market

Commercial News 193

The stationery department of the Wing On Company announced that foreign movie star photographs had arrived from the United States, including full-length and half-length portraits in various styles, mostly in color, priced at 13 cents each or $1.50 per dozen. There were also large-sized star photos, 9.5 inches high and 7 inches wide, priced at 60 cents each. At the same time, a large number of new-style Conklin fountain pens arrived in various styles, priced from $7.10, $9.50 to $32.50 each. Two-way pens were available at $18.20 and $20.08 each.

The Central Grand Hotel on Wuma Road, Zhenfeng Street, announced that they had added a storytelling venue with two sessions, day and night, with five storytellers in each session. The finale will feature comedic performances. Preparations have been underway for several months, and in planning the seating for the audience, they have sacrificed spaciousness to reduce the number of seats, specially making spacious chairs to ensure that listeners are comfortable and do not feel the discomfort of cramped seating. They have hired storytellers from various schools of storytelling, such as Yang Xiaoting and Zhao Xiaoqing, father and son, and Jiang Yifei, as well as three performers: Jiang Binchu, Wang Xiang, and Wang Siquan. Comedic performers such as Wang Wuneng, Cheng Jingping, and Guan Mitang are all well-known and top-notch talents of the time. There will also be a group of eight famous comedians performing a spoken play, which has never been performed in any entertainment venue in Shanghai. The opening is approaching and is sure to create a sensation.

A magnificent new building has been constructed at the corner of Aiduo Road and Dongxin Bridge in the French Concession. The four-story building is beautiful and extremely impressive. A fully equipped, large-scale bicycle shop will be opened there. Preparations are currently underway and business will begin as soon as everything is ready.

Medical News 194

Dr. Wu Guoqing announced that he has studied medicine abroad and is skilled in medical arts. He is now practicing medicine in Shanghai. He is able to cure any critical illness with just one diagnosis. He also provides free medical treatment to poor households who come to him for treatment.

Yushangchu, a medical practitioner at Ximen Xie Bridge, announced that his "Yushi All-Purpose Effective Plaster" is specially supplied for charitable purposes. Regardless of gender or age, the plaster is effective for all kinds of diseases and ailments. Yang Jun Shao Hou and He Jun Wuliang have commissioned tens of thousands of plasters each year to be distributed to poor people in the countryside and in Shanghai, relieving the suffering of tens of thousands of people. The medical practitioner also has a charitable heart and will only charge the cost of the medicine for those who purchase or commission the plasters.

Nankui Hospital at 27 Baker Road announced that Dr. Liu Dongxing, the director of the hospital, has always been known for his charitable heart. To help the poor with their illnesses, the consultation fee is only ten copper coins. The consultation hours are from 8:00 AM to 11:30 AM. The remaining time is for general outpatient services.

Publishing News 195

Caoyeshe, located at 34 Feilun Road, announced that the 11th issue of the second volume of the Caoye Weekly will be published on the 14th. It is a special issue featuring works by famous modern Chinese writers, including Yu Baimang's Nostalgia, Bai Lunwang Tiehua's Boating on Turtle Head Isle, Tang Zenghui's Autumn Deepens, My Girl, and several literary news items from Nuofu et al., totaling twelve articles. All newspaper vendors are authorized to sell it.

Calligraphy and Painting News 196

Li Shizhou was a Jinshi (successful candidate in the highest imperial examination) during the Gengzi year of the late Qing Dynasty and served as an official in Guangxi. He loves calligraphy and has studied the works of the Han, Wei, Six Dynasties, Tang, and Song dynasties from childhood to old age for over forty years without interruption. Therefore, his works are grand, ancient, simple, vigorous, extraordinary, and free from vulgarity. Now, Mr. Li is traveling and creating calligraphy in Shanghai, leaving his mark behind. Those who wish to obtain Mr. Li's calligraphy can contact Yi Ji Zhan at Dai Gou Qiao. Prices will be sent upon request by mail.

The painter Huang Xiao Chi announced that his residence is located at No. 5, Xinxingshun Lane, Ganshi East Road, French Concession. Due to the remote location, he has entrusted the Yichuntang paper and fan shop at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Wangping Street as the general receiving point for works. Landscape paintings are temporarily sold at 60% of the original price to expand his network and a figure painting is included as a gift. For paintings commissioned by the foot, each foot costs only $1.20 (limited to five feet). Folding screens are sold at 60% of the original price, and fan paintings are calculated as one foot each. All fan shops are authorized to receive commissions. Patrons are welcome to visit.

Theater News 197

The Gongming Singing and Dancing Music Research Association announced that it has been preparing for its fourth public performance for nearly two months. Yesterday was its sixth general meeting, with over fifty attendees. It was decided that a gathering for new and old members would be held this Saturday at the Chen Garden in Jiangwan. The leaders of each district, Ying Ying, Yu Lin, Yu Zhen, Man Li, Man Lin, Lu Xi, Qiu Xia, and Yi Wen, will be responsible for the event. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM.

5 (5) Youth Garden

A Conversation with Athletes After Returning from the Greater East Asia Games 198

Several individuals were selected as representatives for this year's Far Eastern Games and the Greater East Asia Games, including Cao Yu, Hao Chunde, Zhong Lianji, Feng Yunyou, Dai Linjing, Chen Zhenhe, and Chen Jiaqiu. These representatives returned to the country the day before yesterday and arrived safely at the school. The school authorities inquired about the reasons for the failure this time and their feelings after going to Japan. A brief record is as follows:

It is said that the most heartbreaking thing for our country is football, because football has always been something we were expected to win, like taking something out of a pocket. Unexpectedly, it ended in a tie, which was truly unimaginable. The main reason for the failure is that the talent is unevenly distributed and the lack of practice made it impossible to connect. For example, Uncle Gong (Feng Yunyou's nickname), who is known for his good defense, was transferred to the front line to charge into battle, which was not his strength. Also, the absence of Li Qiuwai also detracted from the team's performance. Although the Japanese are a short nation, their players are not short. Their height has a certain size and a corresponding physique, unlike our country, where it is random. The Japanese can encourage hard work, so they have made such amazing progress, which our people cannot match. The unfairness of the refereeing is also a major reason. As for the failures in other aspects such as track and field and basketball, on the one hand, there is a lack of practice, and on the other hand, some people participate in too many events and do not have the energy, resulting in nothing being achieved.

As for those who asked the athletes for autographs, they were overwhelmed. Not only did they want Chinese autographs, but also English ones. Some athletes were good at Chinese autographs, and some were good at English ones, but it was rare to find someone who could do both well. On the one hand, this shows the enthusiasm and curiosity of the Japanese people for sports.

When asked why Ms. Sun Guiyun of the健而美 team was not selected, it was said that she was too impatient and did not understand the language, which was the cause of her problem. She was disqualified only on the fourth time she violated the rules, and the judges had already given her a chance. Finally, the athletes said that they deeply understood that this failure is the mother of success. As the saying goes (Don't get angry, just remember). If the people of the country work hard and practice more, and at the same time, the government, schools, and the public strongly promote it, the future four years will be different from today. Although the statements are ordinary, they are enough to inspire the will of young people, so I have made a special record of them. (An) Yang Zeheng.

Ms. Yang Heng Won the Women's Tennis Championship at the Education College of Jinan University This Year 199

The first teachers and students' joint sports meeting of the Education College of Jinan University ended the week before last. The meeting included tennis, basketball, football, volleyball, and track and field competitions. Tennis was divided into men's and women's groups, while the rest were mixed. Ms. Yang Heng, who won the women's singles tennis championship this year, also represented the school last year in the Mandarin speech competition for all universities in Shanghai and the four universities in Jiangnan and won both first prizes. It is reported that Ms. Yang's health has been poor since returning to the country, and she has felt very weak. Therefore, she gave up her specialty of speech (it is a pity that Jinan University lost this competition because Ms. Yang was weak and did not participate) and engaged in physical education. She practices on the tennis court every morning and has achieved great results. According to those close to Ms. Yang, her health has gradually recovered and her complexion has improved since she paid attention to exercise. We hope that Ms. Yang will practice more and become not only an educator, speaker, and playwright, but also a physical education expert. (An)

Professor's Utensil 200

Ms. Bland, a professor at Aurora University, is usually very popular with students. During the school's fifth-anniversary celebration, she trained some male and female students in the university to perform English plays and dances. During the training period, she was very satisfied and confident that she would not fail.

But on the night of the performance of the English play, the audience suddenly made a strange noise and started shouting one after another. Not only were the performers flustered, but the director was also anxious. At first, she thought the actors had made a mistake, but after careful observation, there were no mistakes at all.

When the dance was performed, the audience made the same strange noise. This time, she was extremely angry and returned to the dormitory where she cried to the female students, saying, "I have directed students to perform plays many times, and I have never been subjected to such stimulation. And especially in a high-level and rigorous academic institution!" After saying that, she kept crying for two nights. The female students who were trained by her had worked hard for almost a month, and not only did they not receive praise, but they also added a lot of cold ridicule from the students. They couldn't help but shed tears of sympathy with Ms. Bland. (Bi)
